рд╡рд┐рд╕реНрддрд╛рд░рдГ (рджреНрд░рд╖реНрдЯреБрдВ рдиреЛрджреНрдпрдореН)

Description by Mark S.G. Dyczkowski:

The Kriyakramadyotika by Aghora┼Ыiv─Бc─Бrya who lived in South India in the 12th century, is the primary ritual manual which guides ritual procedure in most of the major ┼Ыaiva temples of South India. This is a major commentary on it by Kacchepe┼Ыvara who lived in K─Б├▒c─л. At the beginning he refers to Aghora┼Ыiva as his teacher telling us that he wrote it impelled by his grace.
